<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Stores the last execution point shown by the revSEGoExecutionPoint command. This is</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># used when coming out of debug mode to deselect the highilighted line if the user has</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># not changed it.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> sLastShownExecutionPoint</font></p>

<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pStartingLine : optional line number to seek to.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Sets the current object to edit to pObject. If pStartingLine is given, then seeks to that line</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   otherwise seeks to the last selected line.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">command</font></b><font color="#000000"> revSESetCurrentObject pObject, pStartingLine, pDontSendCallbacks</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">lock</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">screen</font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># added to the script editor.</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># OK-2008-11-24 : Bug 7477 - If the object is on a password protected stack, this could throw an error,</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># we catch this, and simply don't set the checksum here. Instead it will be set when the script is unlocked.</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>try</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tScript</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">script</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> tObject </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tScript</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      seUpdateChecksum tObject, tScript</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>try</b></font></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">end</font></b><font color="#000000"> revSEAddTargetObject</font></p>
<p></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Parameters</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pObject : reference to the object to remove</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pDontWarn : whether or not to warn the user of losing unapplied changes (optional, defaults to false)</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pDontCloseIfLast : optional, defaults to false. If true, then the script editor will not be closed when the last tab is deleted.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pDontChangeTab : optional, defaults to false, If true, then the script editor will not attempt to change tabs after removing the object</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Removes the specified object from this script editor. If the removed object is the current</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   editing object, then changes the current object to the last selected object.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">command</font></b><font color="#000000"> revSERemoveTargetObject pObject, pDontWarn, pDontCloseIfLast, pDontChangeTab</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tState</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> seGetObjectState(pObject) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tState</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> pDontWarn </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">not</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">true</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">and</font><font color="#000000"> (tState </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"edited"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">or</font><font color="#000000"> (tState </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"error"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">and</font><font color="#000000"> revIDEObjectIsOnIDEStack(pObject))) <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      revSEWarnBeforeClosing pObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>if</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">result</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"cancel"</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         <b>exit</b> revSERemoveTargetObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#007F00"># re-initialize the script editor. This situation can happen if the script editor is reload objects in response to a </font></b></p>

<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"initialize"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Editor"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>else</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#007F00"># This means the last tab has been closed. In this case, we just close the script editor.</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         seFinalize</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"revSEDeleteSubStack the long id of me"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">stack</font><font color="#000000"> (</font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">mainstack</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font><font color="#000000">) </font><font color="#7F007F">in</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">0</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">milliseconds</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">close</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># Note that the cache for the old object is removed after the object has been changed to the new one,</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># this is because changing the object in normal circumstances saves the cache of the previous object. Here however</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># we wish the cache to be cleared because we are removing the object rather than just switching tabs.</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"clearCache pObject, tTrueString"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Editor"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">there</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">a</font><font color="#000000"> pObject <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      seSetObjectState pObject, </font><font color="#00007F">"applied"</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>else</b>   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># OK-2008-09-11 : Only cancel pending messages if the object no longer exists, otherwise </font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># gutter updates will be lost without cause.</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># Any pending messages must be cancelled as they may refer to the deleted object</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"cancelPendingMessages"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Editor"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">end</font></b><font color="#000000"> revSERemoveTargetObject</font></p>
<p></p>
<p><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> sMode</font></p>
<p></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Returns the current mode of this script editor. The possible options are</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   "edit" and "debug".</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">command</font></b><font color="#000000"> revSEGetMode</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># The mode will be stored in a script local variable, just return this.</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> sMode </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">empty</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"edit"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> sMode</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">return</font></b><font color="#000000"> sMode</font></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">end</font></b><font color="#000000"> revSEGetMode</font></p>
<p></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Parameters</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pMode : the mode to set to, either "edit" or "debug"</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Sets the mode of this script editor.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">command</font></b><font color="#000000"> revSESetMode pMode</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># Note, sMode should be set first because the various update messages</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># sent to components may check the mode, and we want them to update</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># according to the new mode, not the old one.</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> pMode </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> sMode</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> pMode </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"edit"</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"scriptUnlock"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Editor"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># This means if a line was selected by the debugger to show the user where the current</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># execution point was, it will be deselected here. If the user selected something themselves,</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># this will not be effected.</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"deselectLastGoneToLine"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Editor"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      sePrefSet </font><font color="#00007F">"debug,lastcontext"</font><font color="#000000">, </font><font color="#7F007F">empty</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> pMode </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"debug"</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"scriptLock"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Editor"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># If in debug mode, we default to the variables pane for convenience</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tLastSelectedPane</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> pMode </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Debug"</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Variables"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tLastSelectedPane</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>else</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> sePrefGet(pMode &amp; </font><font color="#00007F">",lastSelectedPane"</font><font color="#000000">) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tLastSelectedPane</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># Update the window title</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   revSEGetCurrentObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">result</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> tObject </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">not</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">empty</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      seUpdateWindowTitle tObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"setCurrentTab tLastSelectedPane"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Pane Tabs"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"update"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Toolbar"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   actionResizeStack</font></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">end</font></b><font color="#000000"> revSESetMode</font></p>
<p></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Parameters</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pPrefsChanged : whether or not the script editor preferences have changed or not, if empty, assumes they *have* changed.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Updates the script editor menu, toolbar and panes etc in response to something</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   changing, eg execution context.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">command</font></b><font color="#000000"> revSEUpdate pPrefsChanged</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># Reinitialize the preferences in case they have been changed</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> pPrefsChanged </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">not</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"false"</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      sePrefInit</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># If the debug context has changed, update it</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00">--   if sMode is "debug" then</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00">--      local tCurrentContext</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00">--      put line 1 of seDebugContexts() into tCurrentContext</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00">--      sePrefSet "debug,lastcontext", tCurrentContext</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00">--   end if</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"update"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Toolbar"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"refreshCurrentPane"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Panes"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># Breakpoints might have been disabled or removed, so update the gutter</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tEmptyString</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">empty</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tEmptyString</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tTrueString</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"true"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tTrueString</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"false"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tFalseString</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"updateGutterRequest tEmptyString, tEmptyString, tEmptyString, tEmptyString, tFalseString, tFalseString, tTrueString"</font><font color="#000000">  </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Editor"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> pPrefsChanged </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">not</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"false"</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      seUpdateLeftBar</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"reapplyPreferences"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Editor"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"reapplyPreferences"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Variables"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>

<p><b><font color="#000000">end</font></b><font color="#000000"> revSEUpdate</font></p>
<p></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Parameters</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pObject : reference to the object executing. Must be an open object in the script editor.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pLine : the line number to go to</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pHighlight : whether to highlight the line or not</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pOpenIfNeeded : if true, the open is opened by the script editor if required.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Goes to the execution point specified by pObject and pLine. The line is highlighted</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   if pHighlight is true. If pObject is not one of the current target objects does nothing.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">command</font></b><font color="#000000"> revSEGoExecutionPoint pObject, pLine, pHighlight, pOpenIfNeeded</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tTargetObjects</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   revSEGetTargetObjects</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">result</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tTargetObjects</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> seGetRuggedId(pObject) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> tObject </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">not</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">among</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">lines</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> tTargetObjects <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># Either open tObject or do nothing</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>if</b> pOpenIfNeeded <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         revSEAddTargetObject tObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>else</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         <b>exit</b> revSEGoExecutionPoint</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   revSESetCurrentObject tObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"goLine pLine, pHighlight"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Editor"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> pLine </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> sLastShownExecutionPoint</font></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">end</font></b><font color="#000000"> revSEGoExecutionPoint</font></p>
<p></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Returns the last selected string in the editor group</font></b></p>

<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"findFinalize"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Editor"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>

<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Parameters</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pQuery : the string to search for</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pIsRegExp : whether or not pQuery is a regular expression</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pUseWildCards : whether or not to treat *s as wildcards</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pIgnoreCase : whether to do a case sensitive search or not</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pTarget : whether to search in all tabs or just the current tab</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Searches for the next match according to the specified search criteria. Highlights the match if found.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">command</font></b><font color="#000000"> revSEFindNext pQuery, pIsRegExp, pUseWildCards, pWholeMatch, pIgnoreCase, pTarget</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"showNextFindResult pQuery, pIsRegExp, pUseWildCards, pWholeMatch, pIgnoreCase, false, pTarget"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Editor"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">end</font></b><font color="#000000"> revSEFindNext</font></p>

<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Parameters</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pQuery : the string to search for</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pIsRegExp : whether or not pQuery is a regular expression</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pUseWildCards : whether or not to treat *s as wildcards</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pIgnoreCase : whether to do a case sensitive search or not</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pTarget : whether to search in all tabs or just the current tab</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pCallback : optional. The name of a command to send with a message saying what state the search is in</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Searches for all matches for the specified search and displays them in the "Search Results" pane.</font></b></p>

<p><b><font color="#007F00"># OK-2008-08-19 : Bug 6947 - Store script checksums to detect whether the user has modified the script externally.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> sScriptChecksums</font></p>
<p></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Parameters</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pObject : reference to the object that had its rugged id changed.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pOldRuggedId : the old rugged id of the object</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Sent when something has caused the rugged if of an object being edited by this script editor to change.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   There are two cases when this happens:</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#      1. The user changes the id of an image that is having its script edited</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#      2. The user changes the mainstack of the stack that owns (or is) one of the objects being edited.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Updates the script editor by changing stored references to the object and any UI elements that</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   are displaying parts of the object's rugged id.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">command</font></b><font color="#000000"> revSEObjectRuggedIdChanged pObject, pOldRuggedId</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> seGetRuggedId(pObject) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tObjectList</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   revSEGetTargetObjects</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">result</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tObjectList</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>repeat</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">for</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">each</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">line</font><font color="#000000"> tTargetObject </font><font color="#7F007F">in</font><font color="#000000"> tObjectList</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>if</b> (tTargetObject </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> pOldRuggedId) </font><font color="#7F007F">or</font><font color="#000000"> (seRuggedObjectContainsObject(pOldRuggedId, tTargetObject)) <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tNewId</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         <b>if</b> tTargetObject </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> pOldRuggedId <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">            </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> tObject </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tNewId</font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">            </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> tTargetObject </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tNewId</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">            </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">replace</font></b><font color="#000000"> pOldRuggedId </font><font color="#7F007F">with</font><font color="#000000"> tObject </font><font color="#7F007F">in</font><font color="#000000"> tNewId</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>

<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Parameters</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pObjectList : a list of the objects that are being closed</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Prompts the user to find out if they want to save changes in the specified list of edited</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   objects. If the user answers yes, applies the scripts of the objects without showing any</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   errors. If the user answers no, does nothing and returns empty. If the user answers cancel</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   then does nothing and returns "cancel"</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">command</font></b><font color="#000000"> revSEWarnBeforeClosing pObjectList</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> pObjectList </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">empty</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">return</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">empty</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>

<p></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Parameters</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pError : a string representing the execution error, in the standard Revolution format.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pObject : the object that threw the error. If empty, the current script editor object is assumed.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pObject should normally be one of the objects being edited. The script editor will not change the </font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   current object to pObject, this should be done by the caller.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Shows the errors pane with a description of the error.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">command</font></b><font color="#000000"> revSEDisplayExecutionError pError, pObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> pObject </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">empty</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      revSEGetCurrentObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">result</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>else</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> revRuggedId(pObject) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># Because this can be called by the debugger, we must not allow an execution</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># error here or the IDE will be broken. If there is no appropriate object then </font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># we just do nothing.</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> tObject </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">empty</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>exit</b> revSEDisplayExecutionError</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"clearErrors"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Errors"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"addError execution, pError, tObject"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Errors"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"setCurrentTab errors"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Pane Tabs"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"expandCurrentPane"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Panes"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">end</font></b><font color="#000000"> revSEDisplayExecutionError</font></p>
<p></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Parameters</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pObjectList : a list of object references that are being edited by this script editor</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pIgnoreErrors : whether to ignore compilation errors or not. </font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Attempts to compile, then applies each specified script. If pIgnoreErrors is true then</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   does not show any compile errors.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Returns</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Empty if application was successful, a list of scripts that failed otherwise</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">command</font></b><font color="#000000"> revSEApplyAll pObjectList, pIgnoreErrors</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tCompilationErrors, tResult, tFailedScripts</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>repeat</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">for</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">each</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">line</font><font color="#000000"> tObject </font><font color="#7F007F">in</font><font color="#000000"> pObjectList</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      applyScript tObject, pIgnoreErrors, tCompilationErrors</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">result</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tResult</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>if</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">not</font><font color="#000000"> tResult <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#007F00"># This means the script could not be applied due to an execution error. Not sure how to handle this,</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#007F00"># but the most sensible choice seems to be to cancel the closure and allow the user to see the error.</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> tObject &amp; </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">return</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">after</font><font color="#000000"> tFailedScripts</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>repeat</b></font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">return</font></b><font color="#000000"> tFailedScripts</font></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">end</font></b><font color="#000000"> revSEApplyAll</font></p>

<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Stores whether or not the script editor has been suspended by the "Suspend Development Tools" IDE function.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># This has to be stored because if the script editor is a modeless or palette window, the engine will send preOpenStack</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># and related messages to it when restored, regardless of whether messages are locked. Keeping track of whether </font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># the script editor is suspended allows us to disregard these messages.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> sSuspended</font></p>
<p></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Called just before the script editor is about to be suspended (by suspend development tools menu item)</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Prepares the script editor for this.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">command</font></b><font color="#000000"> revSESuspend</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">set</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">destroyStack</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">false</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">true</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> sSuspended</font></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">end</font></b><font color="#000000"> revSESuspend</font></p>

<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Returns</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   A list of the debug contexts available to this script editor. This is the same as the list returned</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   by the debugger library except without any contexts with this stack as their target. This means</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   that it is not possible to debug the script editor in the same instance that is being debugged,</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   but does not prevent debugging using a different instance. revLibrary should reflect this by</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   not allowing a script editor to edit its own scripts, but forcing a new instance.</font></b></p>

<p><b><font color="#007F00"># OK-2009-01-17 : Bug 7169 - Semantics changed slightly. Previously this command returned a list</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># of all unapplied scripts. Now it only returns unapplied scripts that were modified by the user.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># The situation where this makes a difference is when the script contains a template automatically</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># filled in by the script editor. In this context, such a script is no longer viewed as modified.</font></b></p>
<p></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Returns</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   A list of the target objects with unapplied changes to their scripts that were made by the user.</font></b></p>

<p></p>
<p><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> sObjectStates</font></p>
<p></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Parameters</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pObject : reference to one of the target objects of the script editor.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Returns</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   The state of the script of the specified object. This can</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   currently either be "edited" "applied" or "error"</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">function</font></b><font color="#000000"> seGetObjectState pObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tState</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> sObjectStates[seGetRuggedId(pObject)] </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tState</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> tState </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">empty</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"applied"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tState</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">return</font></b><font color="#000000"> tState</font></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">end</font></b><font color="#000000"> seGetObjectState</font></p>
<p></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Parameters</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pObject : reference to one of the target objects of the script editor.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pState : either "edited" or "applied"</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Stores the specified state for the object for later use. And updates any</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   script editor components that may depend on this information.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">command</font></b><font color="#000000"> seSetObjectState pObject, pState</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> pState </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"edited"</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tObj</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">long</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">id</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> pObject </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tObj</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>if</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">not</font><font color="#000000"> revIDEObjectIsOnIDEStack(tObj) <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tParams</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">text</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">field</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Script"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tParams[</font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000">]</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> tObj </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tParams[</font><font color="#00007F">2</font><font color="#000000">]</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"ideMessageSendWithParameters"</font><font color="#000000"> &amp;&amp; </font><font color="#00007F">"ideScriptEdited, tObj, tParams"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">stack</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"revIDELibrary"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">in</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">0</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">milliseconds</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># Small optimization, if pState is equal to the current state, don't do anything</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> pState </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> sObjectStates[seGetRuggedId(pObject)] <b>then</b></font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"refreshTabStates"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Script Tabs"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tId</font></p>

<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Minimum height to attempt to keep the editor above. This is not a "hard" limit,</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># if the user continues shrinking the stack eventually the editor will be smaller than this</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># but the script editor will resize other objects in order to attempt to preserve this.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#7F7F00">constant</font></b><font color="#000000"> kEditorMinimumHeight = </font><font color="#00007F">100</font></p>

<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Line 1 is whether the breakpoint should be displayed as active or not, (i.e will it actually trigger?)</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Line 2 is whether the breakpoint is on a valid line or not</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Line 3 is a string explaining the breakpoint's status, suitable for displaying to the user. This will be empty if the breakpoint is active.</font></b></p>

<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># Find out if the breakpoint is active or not. This is linear to the number of breakpoints</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># in the worst case, so may need to be optimized somehow.</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tBreakpointState</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> tLineNumber = </font><font color="#00007F">0</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># If the breakpoint is not known then it must be a user added one, in this case</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># we just assume that its state is "active".</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"active"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tBreakpointState</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>else</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>if</b> tObjectIsBeingEdited </font><font color="#7F007F">and</font><font color="#000000"> seGetObjectState(tObject) </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">not</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"applied"</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"inactive"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tBreakpointState</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>else</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">line</font><font color="#000000"> tLineNumber </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> tStates </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tBreakpointState</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         <b>if</b> tBreakpointState </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"inactive"</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">            </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">return</font></b><font color="#000000"> (</font><font color="#00007F">"inactive"</font><font color="#000000"> &amp; </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">return</font></b><font color="#000000"> &amp; </font><font color="#00007F">"false"</font><font color="#000000"> &amp; </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">return</font></b><font color="#000000"> &amp; </font><font color="#00007F">"this breakpoint is currently disabled"</font><font color="#000000">)</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tScript</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> tObjectIsBeingEdited <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"scriptGet tObject"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Editor"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">result</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tScript</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>else</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">script</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> tObject </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tScript</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tBreakpointInvalid</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">false</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tBreakpointInvalid</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> revDebuggerNextAvailableBreakpoint(tScript, pLine - </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000">) &lt;&gt; pLine <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"inactive"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tBreakpointState</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">true</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tBreakpointInvalid</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tMessage</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> tObjectIsBeingEdited </font><font color="#7F007F">and</font><font color="#000000"> seGetObjectState(tObject) </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">not</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"applied"</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"this breakpoint will not trigger because the script has not been applied or contains errors"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tMessage</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>else</b> <b>if</b> tBreakpointInvalid <b>then</b></font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>

<p></p>
<p><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> sHistory</font></p>
<p></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Parameters</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pObject : reference to an object whose script was edited</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Adds the specified object to the script editor history</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">command</font></b><font color="#000000"> seHistoryAdd pObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">number</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">lines</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> sHistory &gt;= sePrefGet(</font><font color="#00007F">"historysize"</font><font color="#000000">) <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># First remove any non-existing objects, if there is still no room, remove the last item on the list</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      seHistoryClean</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>if</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">number</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">lines</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> sHistory &gt;= sePrefGet(</font><font color="#00007F">"historysize"</font><font color="#000000">) <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         seHistoryRemove (</font><font color="#7F007F">line</font><font color="#000000"> -1 </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> seHistoryGet())</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> sHistory </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">empty</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> seGetRuggedId(pObject) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> sHistory</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>else</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> seGetRuggedId(pObject) &amp; </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">return</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">before</font><font color="#000000"> sHistory</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">end</font></b><font color="#000000"> seHistoryAdd</font></p>
<p></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Parameters</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pObject : reference to the object to remove from the history</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Removes the specified object from the history list. Leaving the order of other items as it was</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">command</font></b><font color="#000000"> seHistoryRemove pObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># Just to avoid error messages when working on the template</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">there</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">no</font><font color="#000000"> pObject <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>exit</b> seHistoryRemove</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tLineNumber</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">lineOffset</font><font color="#000000">(seGetRuggedId(pObject), sHistory) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tLineNumber</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> tLineNumber = </font><font color="#00007F">0</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>exit</b> seHistoryRemove</font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">delete</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">line</font><font color="#000000"> tLineNumber </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> sHistory</font></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">end</font></b><font color="#000000"> seHistoryRemove</font></p>

<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Parameters</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pType : the type of breakpoint that we are editing. This is either "breakpoint" or "watch"</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pLine : the line number (if pType is "breakpoint", otherwise ignored)</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pVariable : the name of the variable (if pType is "watch", otherwise ignored)</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pHandler : the name of the handler containing the variable (if pType is "watch", otherwise ignored)</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pCondition : the condition attached to the breakpoint (both types)</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pObject : the object that the watch or breakpoint is associated with.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Desription</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Shows the edit breakpoint dialog. (This is the same as the new breakpoint one, but with different properties set.)</font></b></p>

<p><b><font color="#000000">end</font></b><font color="#000000"> seFriendlyShortcut</font></p>
<p></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Parameters</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pText : the word to search for, note this is not necessarily a handler name</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pObject : reference to the object containing the text</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pHandler : the handler that the matching text was found in in the form &lt;type&gt;,&lt;name&gt; (or empty)</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Returns</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   A list, one per line, of the matching handler definitions</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   for pText. Empty if none could be found.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Note that for now, only handler definitions are returned.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">function</font></b><font color="#000000"> seMatchingDefinitions pText, pObject, pHandler</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># Handler name lookups must be case-insensitive: LiveCode handler names are</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># case-insensitive, so a call-site spelling like "myhandler" must match a</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># definition stored as "myHandler". Also ensures `is` comparisons for object</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># long IDs are caseless. Save/restore so we don't affect the caller.</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tSavedCaseSensitive</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">caseSensitive</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tSavedCaseSensitive</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">set</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">caseSensitive</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">false</font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># right-clicked on a definition or a call-site in the object being edited.</font></b></p>

<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># handlers from other objects in the path. When pObject is itself a behavior</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># (tUses[1] exists) use its first user as the anchor for the effective path;</font></b></p>

<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00">-- The effective revScriptDescription approach fails when the anchor object</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00">-- (processed with p_include_all=true) has the engine bug. Multiple objects</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00">-- in this stack appear to be affected, so instead walk the owner chain</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00">-- manually, checking each object with revScriptDescription and falling back</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00">-- to script-text scanning when that also fails.</font></b></p>
<p></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00">-- First try the effective description of tObject (works when tObject != pObject,</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00">-- e.g. when pObject is a behavior script used by another object).</font></b></p>

<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00">-- Effective description failed. Walk the ancestor chain by parsing</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00">-- pObject's long id, which yields fully-qualified references at every</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00">-- level (e.g. "group id N of card id M of stack id K", then</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00">-- "card id M of stack id K", then "stack id K"). This avoids the</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00">-- short-form owner references that `the owner of X` returns and that</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00">-- the engine cannot resolve as standalone object identifiers.</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tCurrentObject, tCurrentDesc, tDescErr2</font></p>

<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Called when the script editor stack is resized. First resizes each script editor object,</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   then sends a "resize" message to each object to allow the object to resize its controls</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   appropriately to its new size.</font></b></p>

<p></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Parameters</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pObject : the object to apply the script of</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pIgnoreErrors : causes errors in setting the script not to be displayed in the errors pane and IDE scripts to be set regardless of errors</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   @rCompilationErrors : gets the list of compilation errors placed into it. Will be set to empty if none occurred.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Returns</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   True if the script was applied, false otherwise. Note that compilation errors may occur but the script could </font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   still be applied. Possible reasons for failure are that the script being applied is executing, on the stack's cantModify is true.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Attempts to set the script of the specified object to the most recent copy in this instance of the script editor. </font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   If setting the script failed due to an execution error, displays the error in the script editor errors pane (unless pIgnoreErrors is true).</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">private</font></b><font color="#000000"> <b>command</b> applyScript pObject, pIgnoreErrors, @rCompilationErrors</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tCompilationResult</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">send</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"scriptCompile pObject"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Editor"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">result</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tCompilationResult</font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># OK-2008-08-20 : All scripts end in return in the engine, we add the return here so that tScript</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># will match what the actual script gets set to. This ensures that we can store correct checksums for scripts.</font></b></p>

<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Parameters</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pIgnoreErrors : whether or not to ignore compilation errors (optional, defaults to false)</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Returns</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   the number of compilation errors encountered.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Attempts to compile the script of object currently being edited. If compile errors occur, adds these to the errors pane,</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   the script is applied regardless of whether errors ocurred or not. The stack is marked as edited.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">command</font></b><font color="#000000"> actionCompile pIgnoreErrors</font></p>

<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Performs the "save" action, saving the stack that owns the current object</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">command</font></b><font color="#000000"> actionSave</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   revSEGetCurrentObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">result</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tStack</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> revTargetStack(tObject) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tStack</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> tStack </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">not</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">empty</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>if</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">effective</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">filename</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">stack</font><font color="#000000"> tStack </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">not</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">empty</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         revSave tStack</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>else</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         revSaveAs tStack</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">end</font></b><font color="#000000"> actionSave</font></p>

<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Saves the stack that the current editing script is owned by, first applying all open scripts which are contained within that stack.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">command</font></b><font color="#000000"> actionApplyAndSave</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># OK-2008-12-20: Bug 7511 - Previously this action only applied the current script, now it applies all scripts in the stack being saved.</font></b></p>

<p><font color="#000000">   revSEGetCurrentObject</font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tTargetObjects</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   revSEGetTargetObjects</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">result</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tTargetObjects</font></p>
