<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tIgnoreErrors = </font><font color="#7F007F">false</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>repeat</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">for</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">each</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">line</font><font color="#000000"> tTargetObject </font><font color="#7F007F">in</font><font color="#000000"> tTargetObjects</font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">         compileScript tTargetObject, tIgnoreErrors</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tCompilationErrors</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">result</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tCompilationErrors</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         <b>if</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">not</font><font color="#000000"> tIgnoreErrors </font><font color="#7F007F">and</font><font color="#000000"> tCompilationErrors </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">not</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">empty</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">and</font><font color="#000000"> revIDEObjectIsOnIDEStack(tTargetObject) <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">            </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">answer</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">error</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"The following script has compilation errors. Would you like to ignore errors and apply the script before saving?"</font><font color="#000000"> &amp; </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">return</font></b><font color="#000000"> &amp; </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">long</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">name</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> tTargetObject </font><font color="#7F007F">with</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Ignore Errors"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">or</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Cancel"</font></p>

<p></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   This action does one of two possible things. If we are already debugging, it</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   performs the debugger "Run" function. Continues executing the script</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   that is being debugged until either execution terminates or a breakpoint is reached.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   If we are not already debugging, then the script is compiled, and a message sent to the object</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   in order to begin execution. The message sent and its parameters are stored as metadata on the object</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   and the user can configure them via the actionEditDebugEntry action. If an entry point has not been</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   configured, then a dialog is shown in order to do so.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">command</font></b><font color="#000000"> actionDebugRun</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tMode</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   revSEGetMode</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">result</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tMode</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> tMode </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"debug"</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      revDebuggerRun</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      revSESetMode </font><font color="#00007F">"edit"</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>exit</b> actionDebugRun</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> tMode </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"edit"</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># Attempt to compile the script first, if it doesn't compile then we don't run it.</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      actionCompile</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>if</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">result</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">not</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">empty</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         <b>exit</b> actionDebugRun</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># Next we figure out which handler / parameters we are going to call, if we don't know</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># then show a dialog to allow the user to choose.</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      revSEGetCurrentObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">result</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tObject</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tHandler</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> revMetadataGet(tObject, </font><font color="#00007F">"general"</font><font color="#000000">, </font><font color="#00007F">"debugEntryHandler"</font><font color="#000000">) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tHandler</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tHandlerList</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      revSEGetHandlerList</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">result</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tHandlerList</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>if</b> tHandler </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">empty</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">or</font><font color="#000000"> (</font><font color="#7F007F">lineOffset</font><font color="#000000">((</font><font color="#7F007F">item</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> tHandler &amp; </font><font color="#7F007F">space</font><font color="#000000"> &amp; </font><font color="#7F007F">item</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">2</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> tHandler), tHandlerList) = </font><font color="#00007F">0</font><font color="#000000">) <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         actionEditDebugEntry</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         <b>if</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">result</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"cancelled"</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">            <b>exit</b> actionDebugRun</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># When clicking the run button, the user will expect the "browse" tool to be selected,</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># as otherwise the debugger won't trigger even if there are breakpoints</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">choose</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">browse</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">tool</font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tParameters</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> revMetadataGet(tObject, </font><font color="#00007F">"general"</font><font color="#000000">, </font><font color="#00007F">"debugEntryHandler"</font><font color="#000000">) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tHandler</font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">      </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># From the handler and parameters, form a piece of Revolution code to execute</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># in order to trigger the script to run. This may not always be a "send blah to tObject"</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># style command, because we permit tHandler to be a function, getProp etc.</font></b></p>

<p><b><font color="#007F00">#</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Keyboard shortcut handling</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">################################################################################</font></b></p>
<p></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Parameters</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pKey : the key that the user pressed. This should be the value of the pKey parameter to message triggered</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Returns</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   The name of the key that should be used to search for an associated action</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">private</font></b><font color="#000000"> <b>function</b> shortcutResolveKey pKey</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>switch</b> pKey</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>case</b> </font><font color="#00007F">"65360"</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">return</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"home"</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">break</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>case</b> </font><font color="#00007F">"65367"</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">return</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"end"</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">break</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>default</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">return</font></b><font color="#000000"> pKey</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>end</b> <b>switch</b></font></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">end</font></b><font color="#000000"> shortcutResolveKey</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">  </font></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Parameters</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pKey : the key that was pressed</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pCommandKey : the state of the command / ctrl key</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pOptionKey : the state of the option / alt key</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pShiftKey : the state of the shift key</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pContext : the action context, currently this is the long id of the focusedObject</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Searches for a shortcut that matches the specified input parameters.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   If a shortcut is found, the associated action is returned, else empty</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   is returned.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">private</font></b><font color="#000000"> <b>function</b> shortcutFindAction pKey, pCommandKey, pOptionKey, pShiftKey, pContext</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># List the available shortcut actions</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tActions</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> sePrefList(</font><font color="#00007F">"shortcuts,*"</font><font color="#000000">) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tActions</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tPressedKey</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> shortcutResolveKey(pKey) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tPressedKey</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># Loop through the available actions and attempt to find one that matches the</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># key combination pressed.</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tFoundAction, tKeys</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>repeat</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">for</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">each</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">line</font><font color="#000000"> tAction </font><font color="#7F007F">in</font><font color="#000000"> tActions</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> sePrefGet(tAction) </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tKeys</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># tKeys may contain multiple lines if there is more than one key combination associated</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># with this action. Loop through each and as soon as we find one that matches, choose that action.</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># It is up to the preferences to ensure that no key combination is associated with more than one</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># action. If this situation ocurrs then the first matching action will be executed.</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>repeat</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">for</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">each</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">line</font><font color="#000000"> tKey </font><font color="#7F007F">in</font><font color="#000000"> tKeys</font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">            <b>next</b> <b>repeat</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         <b>end</b> <b>if</b></font></p>

<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Returns</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Whether or not undo is available, i.e something has been changed in the current script</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">function</font></b><font color="#000000"> seUndoAvailable</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># OK-2009-01-17 : Bug 7597 - We have no way of knowing if undo is available for controls</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># other than the editing field, but we assume it *is* available, in order to let it work for other controls.</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>if</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">long</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">id</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">owner</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">focusedObject</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">is</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">long</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#007F7F">id</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Editor"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font><font color="#000000"> <b>then</b></font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">call</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"undoAvailable"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">group</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"Editor"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">me</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">       </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">return</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">the</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">result</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>else</b></font></p>

<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   This handles tabKey based keyboard shortcuts. The only one by default is to switch between tabs</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Note that only command + tab shortcuts are allowed to prevent interference with other functions.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">on</font></b><font color="#000000"> tabKey</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># bhall2001-2017-07-18: Bug 18366 On MacOS, Use control+tab to cycle between tabs</font></b></p>

<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Description</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   This handles return based keyboard shortcuts, along with returnInField. Which one is sent depends on whether a field is focused or not.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   Note that one of the default shortcuts is COMMAND + RETURN, to apply scripts. When the user presses this combination of keys, a returnKey</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   or returnInField is generated, not a commandKeyDown as one might expect.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">on</font></b><font color="#000000"> returnKey</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tAction</font></p>

<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Parameters</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pObject : reference to an object</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pHandler : the specification of a public handler in the script of pObject, in the form &lt;type&gt;,&lt;name&gt;</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   pParameters : a list of parameters, one per line, in the form &lt;name&gt;,&lt;value&gt;</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00"># Returns</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   A piece of Revolution code that can be executed in order to trigger the specified handler in the specified</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#007F00">#   object to run.</font></b></p>
<p><b><font color="#000000">function</font></b><font color="#000000"> buildDebugEntryMessage pObject, pHandler, pParameters</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># Process the parameters. In order to keep things clean and simple, we do this by putting each parameter into a variable</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># and forming two strings, one which declares and populates these variables, and one which contains a list of them to pass</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># to the handler we call. We also create another string which represents the parameters in the form of a revolution expression,</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># this third string is needed to get functions working properly.</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tParameterNumber</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tParameterNumber</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tParameterDeclarations, tParameterString, tParameterExpression</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>repeat</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">for</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">each</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">line</font><font color="#000000"> tParameter </font><font color="#7F007F">in</font><font color="#000000"> pParameters</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"local tParam"</font><font color="#000000"> &amp; tParameterNumber &amp; </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">return</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">after</font><font color="#000000"> tParameterDeclarations</font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#007F00"># Escape quotes from the parameters</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tValue</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">item</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">2</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">to</font><font color="#000000"> -1 </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> tParameter </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tValue</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">replace</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">quote</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">with</font><font color="#000000"> (</font><font color="#7F007F">quote</font><font color="#000000"> &amp; </font><font color="#00007F">" &amp; quote &amp; "</font><font color="#000000"> &amp; </font><font color="#7F007F">quote</font><font color="#000000">) </font><font color="#7F007F">in</font><font color="#000000"> tValue</font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"put "</font><font color="#000000"> &amp; </font><font color="#7F007F">quote</font><font color="#000000"> &amp; tValue &amp; </font><font color="#7F007F">quote</font><font color="#000000"> &amp; </font><font color="#00007F">" into tParam"</font><font color="#000000"> &amp; tParameterNumber &amp; </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">return</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">after</font><font color="#000000"> tParameterDeclarations</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"tParam"</font><font color="#000000"> &amp; tParameterNumber &amp; </font><font color="#7F007F">comma</font><font color="#000000"> &amp; </font><font color="#7F007F">space</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">after</font><font color="#000000"> tParameterString</font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#007F00"># Now the parameters are sorted, generate the command that triggers the entry point.</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">local</font></b><font color="#000000"> tCommandString</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">   <b>switch</b> </font><font color="#7F007F">item</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">1</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> pHandler</font></p>

<p><font color="#000000">      <b>case</b> </font><font color="#00007F">"C"</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#007F00"># event handlers and commands, we can just do a simple "send" to trigger these into action</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#007F00"># we do the send in 0 milliseconds to allow the script editor to fall out of the call stack before the code is executed.</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> tParameterDeclarations &amp; </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">return</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">into</font><font color="#000000"> tCommandString</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">put</font></b><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">"send "</font><font color="#000000"> &amp; </font><font color="#7F007F">quote</font><font color="#000000"> &amp; </font><font color="#7F007F">item</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#00007F">2</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">of</font><font color="#000000"> pHandler &amp;&amp; tParameterString &amp; </font><font color="#7F007F">quote</font><font color="#000000"> &amp; </font><font color="#00007F">" to "</font><font color="#000000"> &amp; pObject &amp; </font><font color="#00007F">" in 0 milliseconds"</font><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#7F007F">after</font><font color="#000000"> tCommandString</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      </font><b><font color="#7F7F00">break</font></b></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">      <b>case</b> </font><font color="#00007F">"F"</font></p>
<p><font color="#000000">         </font><b><font color="#007F00"># functions can be evaluated using the value function, but getting the parameters working is rather tricky...</font></b></p>
